  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_7c63353d-e9fc-4739-a6a9-fe87f270ac94'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_1183899591" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1183899591" />
    <a title="Patrick" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/922495-patrick"><img alt="Patrick" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1351307095p2/922495.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1183899591?book_show_action=true">Jan 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrick" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrick" href="/user/show/922495-patrick">Patrick</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/922495-patrick?shelf=audiobooks">audiobooks</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1183899591" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13850343893586556875">I've yet to be disappointed by any Brandon Sanderson story I've picked up, and this novella continues his winning streak. <br/><br/>This is a cool take on a detective story, and honestly, I'd be surprised if someone in LA hasn't grabbed the rights to turn this into a TV show. It's a show I'd love to watch. <br/><br/>I only have two quibbles with this book, and it only relates to the Audio version, not with the story itself. <br/><br/>1. There were only two tracks on the audio version of the book, each about an hour long. Tha</span>
  <span id="freeText13850343893586556875" style="display:none">I've yet to be disappointed by any Brandon Sanderson story I've picked up, and this novella continues his winning streak. <br /><br />This is a cool take on a detective story, and honestly, I'd be surprised if someone in LA hasn't grabbed the rights to turn this into a TV show. It's a show I'd love to watch. <br /><br />I only have two quibbles with this book, and it only relates to the Audio version, not with the story itself. <br /><br />1. There were only two tracks on the audio version of the book, each about an hour long. That makes for awkward navigation of the book. <br /><br />2. (And I recognize that this is *extra* quibbly) The audio narrator sounded like Bob Newhart to me. <br /><br />Don't get me wrong, he did a good job. He's a pro. But I couldn't get over the fact that his voice sounded like Bob Newhart. I kept thinking, "Wow. He sounds like Bob Newhart." and it would pull me out of the story. <br /><br />But that's probably just my own mental damage, and shouldn't keep you from picking it up, either in print, or on audio... As I said, I really enjoyed it. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13850343893586556875" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8756624673939472348">Another great book by Brandon Sanderson as usual. Insanity, madness and genius go in hand in hand. There is a thin line between each of these and they probably more intersection between them them people want to admit.<br/><br/>Steven Leeds has been call all three. He is a hot property to be studied as he is for his services. When a world changing price of technology goes missing he is recruited to get it back. This is a detective story with a twist on the deductive principle. I really like the clever ways</span>
  <span id="freeText8756624673939472348" style="display:none">Another great book by Brandon Sanderson as usual. Insanity, madness and genius go in hand in hand. There is a thin line between each of these and they probably more intersection between them them people want to admit.<br /><br />Steven Leeds has been call all three. He is a hot property to be studied as he is for his services. When a world changing price of technology goes missing he is recruited to get it back. This is a detective story with a twist on the deductive principle. I really like the clever ways Sanderson show the power of our subconscious mind at work in this story and perceptions as our reality. This is a great little book I can't wait to read the next one.</span>

<div id="review_1115328813" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1115328813" />
    <a title="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8734459-tadiana-night-owl"><img alt="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603085284p2/8734459.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1115328813?book_show_action=true">Nov 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" href="/user/show/8734459-tadiana-night-owl">Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=library-has">library-has</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=the-shorts">the-shorts</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1115328813" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17807443720236747726">Reread as part of Sanderson’s upcoming <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20886354.Skin_Deep__Legion___2_' title='Skin Deep (Legion, #2) by Brandon Sanderson' rel='nofollow noopener'>Skin Deep</a>, which will collect all three Legion novellas (the two previously published ones and a new, concluding one) under one cover. Heads up for NetGalley members: the "Read now" excerpt on NG for <i>Skin Deep</i> consists of this entire first novella, which is kind of nice. So if you haven't read "Legion" and are interested (or just want a copy), grab it!<br/><br/>Upping my rating from 3.5 to 4 stars on reread, because the psychological elements in this story are just s</span>
  <span id="freeText17807443720236747726" style="display:none">Reread as part of Sanderson’s upcoming <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20886354.Skin_Deep__Legion___2_" title="Skin Deep (Legion, #2) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Skin Deep</a>, which will collect all three Legion novellas (the two previously published ones and a new, concluding one) under one cover. Heads up for NetGalley members: the "Read now" excerpt on NG for <i>Skin Deep</i> consists of this entire first novella, which is kind of nice. So if you haven't read "Legion" and are interested (or just want a copy), grab it!<br><br>Upping my rating from 3.5 to 4 stars on reread, because the psychological elements in this story are just so clever and enjoyable.<br><br><i>Legion</i> is a nifty science fiction/mystery novella, with the detective role played by Stephen Leeds and his legion of hallucinatory, brilliant alter egos. In the <i>Skin Deep</i> preface, Sanderson comments:<blockquote>Psychology-as-superpower is a recurring theme in my works. I’ve always believed that the personality traits that make us each distinctive (the way we process information, the way we motivate ourselves, the way we shelter our psyche from the bad while learning to cherish the good) can be either our greatest strengths or our most dramatic limitations…<br><br>The premise was simple: What if a man’s hallucinations proved beneficial to him in his life, rather than the typical distraction?</blockquote>Such a fun concept!<br><br>The mystery in this first story involves a search for a mysterious camera that can take pictures of people and events at any time in the past. Various shadowy groups get involved in the fight to control the camera and its inventor, pulling Stephen Leeds into the case. The time-shifting camera is a device that's been used before in at least a couple of classic SF works that I know of, Isaac Asimov's short story "<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17875715.The_Dead_Past" title="The Dead Past by Isaac Asimov" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dead Past</a>" and "E for Effort," a novella collected in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/219456.The_Science_Fiction_Hall_of_Fame_Volume_II_B__The_Science_Fiction_Hall_of_Fame___2B_" title="The Science Fiction Hall of Fame Volume II B (The Science Fiction Hall of Fame, #2B) by Ben Bova" rel="nofollow noopener">The Science Fiction Hall of Fame: Volume 2B</a>. <i>Legion</i> doesn't really add anything new here, from a science fictional point of view. The story points out some of the problems with the theory of time travel (branching paths of reality; Earth not being in the same place in space as it was in the past you are traveling to, or taking pictures of) ... but it doesn't ever try answer those questions.<br><br>But the real attraction of this story is the main character, Stephen, and the hilarious and colorful cast of <s>characters</s> hallucinations surrounding him: <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427897812ra/14331942.gif" width="250" height="106" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>J.C., the trigger-happy Navy Seal and weapons expert;<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427897812i/14331943.jpg" width="157" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Armando, the trick photography expert who thinks he's the rightful emperor of Mexico;<br><br>Tobias the schizophrenic historian and philosopher; Kalyani the linguist; and so on. Stephen's hallucinations all are brilliant in different fields, all have their own different mental issues, and all are utterly real to him (even though logically he realizes they aren't real, somehow Stephen is able to compartmentalize that realization). Someone points out to Stephen:<blockquote>"You create these delusions so that you can foist things off on them. Your brilliance, which you find a burden. Your responsibility -- they have to drag you along and make you help people. This lets you pretend, Mister Leeds. Pretend you are normal. But that's the <i>real</i> delusion."</blockquote>But real or not, Stephen's legion of invisible experts is a whole lot of fun to read about.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17807443720236747726" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2866860080115577945">Legion (Legion, #1), Brandon Sanderson<br/><br/>Legion is a series of science fiction novellas written by American author Brandon Sanderson. The first book, titled Legion, was first published on August 31, 2012 by Subterranean Press, followed in November 2014 by Legion: Skin Deep, and in September 2018 by Legion: Lies of the Beholder. <br/><br/>Legion tells the story of Stephen Leeds, better known as 'Legion', a man whose unique mental condition allows him to generate multitude of personae. He is a brilliant proble</span>
  <span id="freeText2866860080115577945" style="display:none">Legion (Legion, #1), Brandon Sanderson<br /><br />Legion is a series of science fiction novellas written by American author Brandon Sanderson. The first book, titled Legion, was first published on August 31, 2012 by Subterranean Press, followed in November 2014 by Legion: Skin Deep, and in September 2018 by Legion: Lies of the Beholder. <br /><br />Legion tells the story of Stephen Leeds, better known as 'Legion', a man whose unique mental condition allows him to generate multitude of personae. He is a brilliant problem solver, rich and quite good at what he does, helped by his hallucinations. However, he would rather be left alone, and that means no researchers or psychologists who want to get to the bottom of his abilities. ...<br /><br />تاریخ نخستین خوانش: سال 2012 میلادی<br /><br />عنوان: لژیون؛ براندن ساندرسن؛ مترجم: عماد ذبحی؛ تهران، آذرپاد، 1391؛ در 128 ص؛ شابک: 9786006225333؛ موضوع: داستانهای نویسندگان امریکایی - سده 21 م<br /><br />نقل از آغاز متن: (فصل اول: اسم من «استیفن لیدزه» و من آدم کاملاً سالمی هستم.؛ هرچند توهمات من مطلقاً روانی هستن.؛ صدای شلیک گلوله ای مثل صدای ترقه، از اتاق «جی. سی.» بلند شد.؛ با اینکه زیر لب غرغر میکردم، گوشگیرهایی که پشت در اتاق اون، آویزون کرده بودم رو برداشتم، یاد گرفته بودم که اونها رو اون جا بذارم، و رفتم توی اتاق.؛ «جی.سی.» هم گوشگیرهای خودش رو، به گوشش زده بود، اسلحه ی کمری اش رو دو دستی بالا گرفته بود، و به عکس «اسامه بن لادن»، روی دیوار، زل زده بود.؛ آهنگ «بتهوون»، داشت پخش میشد.؛ با یه صدای شدیداً بلند.؛ داد زدم «مثلاً داشتم با تلفن حرف میزدم!»)؛ پایان نقل<br /><br />تاریخ بهنگام رسانی 01/05/1399هجری خورشیدی؛ ا. شربیانی</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2081083031" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4414617919335767204">Another story that is too short... Damn!!!<br/>I enjoyed Legion. As always, I thought Sanderson’s writing was top notch and not boring. The imagination involved and the detail that went into each of the characters — Stephen Leeds as well as his aspects were astounding. Not only does Legion have a cool plot, but it also has fascinating, multi-faceted characters. Typical Sanderson though, and I definitely mean that in the best possible way.</span>

  <i>Now,</i>
</b>  that <i>was pretty awesome.</i><br/><br/>Wow. <b>Stephen Leeds is the most intriguing and fascinating character I've read about for a very long time</b>. Slightly disturbing - but in a good way, if that's possible, as he kept my interest with his multi-layered personality that we can't easily simplify. Now that I think about it, he gives a whole new meaning to the word <i>multi-layered</i>. <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>"The thing is, I'm really only the reclusive part. And maybe, admittedly,</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText12043863203796105318" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421680142i/13403205._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><u>2015 reads</u> : Give me a flood of crazy people, 'kay?</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Now,</i>
</b>  that <i>was pretty awesome.</i><br><br>Wow. <b>Stephen Leeds is the most intriguing and fascinating character I've read about for a very long time</b>. Slightly disturbing - but in a good way, if that's possible, as he kept my interest with his multi-layered personality that we can't easily simplify. Now that I think about it, he gives a whole new meaning to the word <i>multi-layered</i>. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"The thing is, I'm really only the reclusive part. And maybe, admittedly, the jerk part. When you have that mix, people generally assume you don't have morals either."</b>
</blockquote><br><u>I was hooked at this</u> : <i>"I didn't know what would happen if one of my hallucinations shot me."</i><br><br>Oh, yeah, that's on page <i>two</i>. <b>That was <i>that</i> striking.</b> *nods vigorously* <br><br>Moreover, that was <b>fast-paced</b>, and the thriller kept me enthralled, despite the fact that what enraptured me the most was definitely his hallucinations. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421680142i/13403206._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Can I have some hallucinations too?</i> What? I'm so jealous right now. I totally want : <br><br>- <b>Ivy</b> to tell me if my pupils are lying<br>- <b>Tobias</b> to help me remember of all the books I read - and to help me during some dinners, yes, that would be great. Oh, and he could totally be useful as a travel guide.<br>- <b>Audrey</b> to run writing investigations.<br>- <b>Kalyani</b> or any translator to - well, The possibilities are endless, right?<br>- <b>Armando</b> because. Hum. Not sure I want him actually. I don't think that I have room for Megalomania in my life.<br><br><i>"Can I shoot him?" JC asked me softly. "You know, in a place that's not important? A foot, maybe?"</i><br><br>- <i>Sigh</i>. Yeah, <b>JC</b>, you can come too because you cracked me up. But NO GUNS IN THE HOUSE. No, I don't know how we'll deal with intruders. No, even not that little one. I said no gun. End of story. You can have darts if you want. I know that's not the same thing, I - Oh, whatever. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I'm <i>not</i> going more mad, " I said. "I've stabilized. I'm practically normal. Even my non-hallucinatory psychiatrist acknowledges that."</b>
</blockquote><br>Basically, it is a short story which does not fall into the traps of the lack of characterization or others shortcuts, and that's why I loved it. Oh, and because that was deliciously funny. <br><br><b>What is it that decides you're insane by the way?</b><br><br><i><b><u>Edit</u></b> : For all the French readers out there who want to read in French for a change, I ordered the French version for my BF and you know what? <b>The translation is pretty good</b> (yeah, because that's not always the case, by far). So <b>no excuses.</b> Read it.</i><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><blockquote>

</blockquote></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15754125006962202171">My first Brandon Sanderson book -if we don't count WoT- and I was expecting to be thrown into an epic fantasy world, for some reason. I hadn't read anything about it beforehand.<br/><br/><i>It went more along the lines of this;<br/></i><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486304205ra/21902257.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And caused me to start the story, feeling disoriented.<br/><br/>It was different, well written and didn't feel rushed despite being a novella. I didn't enjoy the story. *it's not you book, it's me* I am left with with no </span>
  <span id="freeText15754125006962202171" style="display:none">My first Brandon Sanderson book -if we don't count WoT- and I was expecting to be thrown into an epic fantasy world, for some reason. I hadn't read anything about it beforehand.<br><br><i>It went more along the lines of this;<br></i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486304205ra/21902257.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And caused me to start the story, feeling disoriented.<br><br>It was different, well written and didn't feel rushed despite being a novella. I didn't enjoy the story. *it's not you book, it's me* I am left with with no wonder, no anger, no feelies. Narrator didn't help either.     <a title="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans"><img alt="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587115780p2/7298986.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" href="/user/show/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans">✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16004601-legion">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=absolute-favourites">absolute-favourites</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=short-stories-novellas">short-stories-novellas</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1095947838" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4300797973085579865"><blockquote>
  <b>"My name is Stephen Leeds, and I'm perfectly sane. My hallucinations, however, are all quite mad."</b>
</blockquote><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420961040ra/13299048.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Brilliant. This is just brilliant. And cool. Very cool. <br/><br/>Do I really have to review this story? It's too awesome for words. You really should just read it.<blockquote>
  <b>“Your hallucination . . .” “Yes?” “Your hallucination has hallucinations.” “Yes.” She settled back, looking disturbed.</b>
</blockquote>Brandon Sanderson I love you. The premise of this story is pure genius.<blockquote>
  <b>“I’m not a hallucination,” J.C. snapped. “I have</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText4300797973085579865" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>"My name is Stephen Leeds, and I'm perfectly sane. My hallucinations, however, are all quite mad."</b>
</blockquote><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420961040ra/13299048.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Brilliant. This is just brilliant. And cool. Very cool. <br><br>Do I really have to review this story? It's too awesome for words. You really should just read it.<blockquote>
  <b>“Your hallucination . . .” “Yes?” “Your hallucination has hallucinations.” “Yes.” She settled back, looking disturbed.</b>
</blockquote>Brandon Sanderson I love you. The premise of this story is pure genius.<blockquote>
  <b>“I’m not a hallucination,” J.C. snapped. “I have state-of-the-art stealthing equipment.”</b>
</blockquote>Legion is about insanity, religion, science, faith… and a very special camera. Mix it all up, shake well, add a good dose of humour, a dash of action and voilà!<blockquote>
  <b>“The truth is, Monica, I don’t want any of this. I’d gladly be free of it, so that I could live a more simple life. I sometimes think the lot of them will drive me insane.” “You . . . aren’t insane, then?” “Heavens no,” I said.</b>
</blockquote>The "lot of them"? The aspects! J.C. the trigger-happy navy seal (I think I'm in love), Ivy the trypophobic therapist, Tobias the schizophrenic historian, Armando the megalomaniac emperor… I love them all.<blockquote>
  <b>“I'm not going more mad,” I said. “I've stabilized. I'm practically normal. Even my non-hallucinatory psychiatrist acknowledges that.”</b>
</blockquote>This was good. Really good. So do yourself a favour and read it.<br><br>· <b>Book 2</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1163170943" rel="nofollow noopener">Skin Deep</a> ★★★★★<br>· <b>Book 3</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1163170943" rel="nofollow noopener">Lies of the Beholder</a> - <i>to be released Sept. 20, 2018</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4298494359407482324">I've been a big fan of Brandon Sanderson for a number of reasons. His excellent Mistborn (he really knows how to develop a magic system and kick off a story with a bang). His participation with readers (such as him stopping in on reddit), his desire to bundle print and ebooks, and for his excellent writing classes (which have been video taped and posted).<br/><br/>So when I heard about this short story I picked it up immediately and read it in a single sitting.   <span id="freeText4298494359407482324" style="display:none">I've been a big fan of Brandon Sanderson for a number of reasons. His excellent Mistborn (he really knows how to develop a magic system and kick off a story with a bang). His participation with readers (such as him stopping in on reddit), his desire to bundle print and ebooks, and for his excellent writing classes (which have been video taped and posted).<br /><br />So when I heard about this short story I picked it up immediately and read it in a single sitting. It was nice seeing the humor of this piece and I thoroughly enjoyed it. Plus it has one of the best opening lines ever..."My name is Stephen Leeds, and I'm perfectly sane. My hallucinations, however, are all quite mad."<br /><br />Some have complained it was too short, I disagree. I think it was the perfect morsel and I look forward for more tidbits in the future.<br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17340422911803950117"><br/>Buddy reading book #2: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20886354.Legion_Skin_Deep__Legion___2_' title='Legion Skin Deep (Legion, #2) by Brandon Sanderson' rel='nofollow noopener'>Legion: Skin Deep</a> tomorrow November 25th with the <b>usual suspects</b>. :) If you still haven't read this one, <b>now is the time</b>!<br/><br/><i>
  <b>4.5 STARS</b>
</i><br/><br/>One of the best opening lines ever:<i> "My name is Stephen Leeds, and I'm perfectly sane. My hallucinations, however, are all quite mad."</i><br/><br/>This was a hilarious read not less amusing than <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17182126.Steelheart__Reckoners___1_' title='Steelheart (Reckoners, #1) by Brandon Sanderson' rel='nofollow noopener'>Steelheart</a> hence the rating I'm giving it.<br/><br/>Stephen Leeds, a.k.a.   <span id="freeText17340422911803950117" style="display:none"><br />Buddy reading book #2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20886354.Legion_Skin_Deep__Legion___2_" title="Legion Skin Deep (Legion, #2) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Legion: Skin Deep</a> tomorrow November 25th with the <b>usual suspects</b>. :) If you still haven't read this one, <b>now is the time</b>!<br /><br /><i>
  <b>4.5 STARS</b>
</i><br /><br />One of the best opening lines ever:<i> "My name is Stephen Leeds, and I'm perfectly sane. My hallucinations, however, are all quite mad."</i><br /><br />This was a hilarious read not less amusing than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17182126.Steelheart__Reckoners___1_" title="Steelheart (Reckoners, #1) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Steelheart</a> hence the rating I'm giving it.<br /><br />Stephen Leeds, a.k.a. "Legion", is a genius whose unique mental condition allows him to generate a multitude of personalities or <i>aspects</i> as he calls them: hallucinatory entities with a wide variety of personal characteristics and a vast array of highly specialized skills(we have an ex-Navy seal /not a marine!:)/ who gives him military action, weapons and strategy advice; a scholar who knows more than any (net) encyclopedia; an Indian linguist and several others no less fascinating ones). As the story begins, Leeds and his 'aspects' are drawn into the search for the missing Balubal Razon, inventor of a camera whose astonishing properties could alter our understanding of human history and change the very structure of society. <br /><br />I very much loved the concept behind this story. I'm always fascinated by the way Sanderson ties religion, or rather faith with science into his books. And this means a lot coming from an atheist like me.<br /><br />I highly recommend the audio. Oliver Wyman did a fantastic job with the different voices and accents for all the characters.</span>

<div id="review_413538124" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/413538124" />
    <a title="seak" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1805180-seak"><img alt="seak" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410456529p2/1805180.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/413538124?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="seak" class="user" itemprop="url" name="seak" href="/user/show/1805180-seak">seak</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781938570018" href="/book/show/16002459-legion">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1805180-seak?shelf=2012">2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer413538124" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1247543726808873585">With Brandon Sanderson, you can always expect something unique and well thought out. It's not even a question. Well, maybe a bit because of that whole finishing the Wheel of Time thing...but otherwise, you can expect what I just said.<br/><br/>That's one of the best parts about reading Sanderson. Yeah, he's got great characters, compelling plot twists and stuff. But what makes him a pleasure to read is the way he makes something like epic fantasy vibrant and new. His unique ideas and magic systems become </span>
  <span id="freeText1247543726808873585" style="display:none">With Brandon Sanderson, you can always expect something unique and well thought out. It's not even a question. Well, maybe a bit because of that whole finishing the Wheel of Time thing...but otherwise, you can expect what I just said.<br /><br />That's one of the best parts about reading Sanderson. Yeah, he's got great characters, compelling plot twists and stuff. But what makes him a pleasure to read is the way he makes something like epic fantasy vibrant and new. His unique ideas and magic systems become characters of their own and half the reason I continue to read is because I want to experience more of it.<br /><br />Legion is no exception. As the novella begins, "My Name is Stephen Leeds, and I am perfectly sane. My hallucinations, however, are all quite mad."<br /><br />Leeds lives in a 47 bedroom mansion inhabited by himself...and his hallucinations. They are each unique, we're lead to believe, but we only deal with a few of them for this story.<br /><br />His hallucinations tend to specialize in different things that help Leeds to be quite the problem solver, which lends well to detective work, not to mention the desire for every shrink in the world to want to study him. <br /><br />The uniqueness to this story is that the hallucinations essentially make Leeds a genius. In some way that is not explained, as long as Leeds takes some time (a very short time actually) to familiarize himself with a particular discipline (such as weapons or linguistics), he will immediately create a hallucination that is an expert in that subject.<br /><br />Having recently read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/323014756" rel="nofollow noopener">The Hollow City</a>, I can't help but wonder who had the idea first. I know Wells and Sanderson are friends. Not that they're exactly the same conept, they just both deal with a protagonist who has hallucinations. This one's much more Sandersonized (of course) with the well thought-out system whereas Wells' seems to be closer to actual schizophrenia. <br /><br />In the end, it's a really fun concept and tons of fun to read, especially when for instance the hallucinations are tied up along with Leeds and one of them frees himself up to untie the rest. Or, when they drive, each of the hallucinations needs their own seat.<br /><br />As if you needed any impetus to read this novella, just do it, have fun, be happy. :)<br /><br />4 out of 5 Stars<br /><br />Note on Rating: While a fun concept (I know, I can't stop saying "fun"), it's not my favorite of his. I can see this concept expanding into more, but I think it really worked well with this shortened format. I think I would have tired of it were it any more. I'm sure I'll have the opportunity to find out.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1247543726808873585" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_842555176" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/842555176" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/842555176?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=super-sidekicks">super-sidekicks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=awesome-audio">awesome-audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=uf-pnr">uf-pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer842555176" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12848288177902813693"><b>4 I see Imaginary People Stars.</b><br/><br/>Quick Re-read before <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20886354.Legion_Skin_Deep__Legion___2_' title='Legion Skin Deep (Legion, #2) by Brandon Sanderson' rel='nofollow noopener'>Legion: Skin Deep</a>is released.<br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> My name is Stephen Leeds, and I am perfectly sane. My hallucinations, however, are all quite mad.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>If that isn’t a great opening line to a story I don’t know what is. Brandon Sanderson is great at thinking outside of the box and congratulations again on coming up with an incredibly unusual premise to write a story on.<br/><br/>I really like that the main character is a functional crazy person. Sure he has hallucina</span>
  <span id="freeText12848288177902813693" style="display:none"><b>4 I see Imaginary People Stars.</b><br /><br />Quick Re-read before <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20886354.Legion_Skin_Deep__Legion___2_" title="Legion Skin Deep (Legion, #2) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Legion: Skin Deep</a>is released.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> My name is Stephen Leeds, and I am perfectly sane. My hallucinations, however, are all quite mad.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />If that isn’t a great opening line to a story I don’t know what is. Brandon Sanderson is great at thinking outside of the box and congratulations again on coming up with an incredibly unusual premise to write a story on.<br /><br />I really like that the main character is a functional crazy person. Sure he has hallucinations but at least he knows they are hallucinations, so how crazy can he actually be. It seems more like he is a genius that has just found a creative way to make compartments for all his knowledge.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “Believe what you will,” I said. “But I’m not a genius. My hallucinations are.”<br />“Thanks,” J.C. said.<br />“Some of my hallucinations are,” I corrected.<br />“You accept that the things you see aren’t real?” Monica said, turning to me.<br />“Yes.”<br />“Yet you talk to them.” <br />“I wouldn’t want to hurt their feelings. Besides, they can be useful.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />This was just a quick mystery of sorts to figure out and a nice introduction into Stephan’s world. The actual mystery was only so/so for me although how much can you pack into less than 100 pages. But, I loved the characters and the weirdness that was Stephan’s mind.<br /><br />I’m intrigued by some hints about his Stephen’s backstory and how perhaps he wasn’t as well adjusted with his hallucinations as he is today. There seems to be a deeper mystery there that I’m hoping Legion: Skin Deep might delve into a little. <br /><br />P.S. The audio version of this was great! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12848288177902813693" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

He is asked to help with a special project that is super awesome...to find it and the man who made it. Super intriguing! <br/>The narrator does a wonderful job with this short novel!</span>

<div id="review_1173556120" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1173556120" />
    <a title="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books"><img alt="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415550632p2/5892196.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1173556120?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" href="/user/show/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books">Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/16065811-legion">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1173556120" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7587517189073951761">This review can also be found at <a href='http://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Carole's Random Life</a>.<br/><br/>4 Stars!<br/><br/>I am quickly becoming a HUGE Brandon Sanderson fan. I only recently become introduced to Sanderson a couple of months ago when I read Steelheart and I am starting to realize that I have really been missing out. This story was completely unique and entertaining. I love how different this story was from anything I have ever encountered before. This story is short but it is highly complex and detailed. <br/><br/>I decided to read this story becaus</span>
  <span id="freeText7587517189073951761" style="display:none">This review can also be found at <a href="http://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Carole's Random Life</a>.<br /><br />4 Stars!<br /><br />I am quickly becoming a HUGE Brandon Sanderson fan. I only recently become introduced to Sanderson a couple of months ago when I read Steelheart and I am starting to realize that I have really been missing out. This story was completely unique and entertaining. I love how different this story was from anything I have ever encountered before. This story is short but it is highly complex and detailed. <br /><br />I decided to read this story because I thought I had the audiobook already in my audible account, I discovered that I actually had the second book in the series so I quickly remedied that situation and started listening right away. I think that the narrator did a fantastic job with this story. He voice was soothing to listen to and he did such a fantastic job with a wide range of characters. <br /><br />Steven Leeds is probably one of the most interesting characters that I have encountered in a book. He is never alone. He lives with his aspects, otherwise known as his hallucinations. Each one of his aspects is an expert in a certain area. Steven claims that he is not a genius and that his aspects are the intelligent one. Of course, he also claims that he isn't crazy and to be honest he acts completely sane if you ignore the fact that he spends most of his time talking to his hallucinations.<br /><br />Steven is quickly enlisted to help locate a missing camera. This isn't just any camera. This camera takes photos that should not exist. When he thinks about what this camera means to society, he feels he has no choice but to try to find it. Steven and his aspects make quite the formidable team as they work to achieve their goal. There are moments in the story when I just need to stop and think for a bit, moments I laughed a little, and other times where I could find out what was going to happen next fast enough. <br /><br />The characters in this story are unbelievably good. Sanderson was able to create a man with a mansion full of hallucinations who appears to be completely sane. Every single aspect that were involved in the story had a distinct personality. While everyone around Steven saw a man talking to nobody, we, the reader, got to see exactly what Steven saw and it was amazing. I never experienced a moment of boredom during the story. Of course, how could I? J.C was running around with guns and hallucinations having hallucinations - I simply had no idea what could possibly be next.<br /><br />I would highly recommend this story to others. I cannot wait to spend more time with Steven and his aspects. I will definitely be reading more from Brandon Sanderson in the not too distant future. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7587517189073951761" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1291629539" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15772200206367312959"><b>Why so shoooort?</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440455796ra/15977126.gif' width='370' height='274' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Legion is a short story about Stephen Leeds who has multiple aspects. <br/><br/><b> <i> My name is Stephen Leeds, and I am perfectly sane. My hallucinations, however, are all quite mad.</i></b><br/><br/>I’m a Sandersonitis for life and when I saw this book in a book sale, I immediately grabbed it. (Of course I paid for it.) I know this book wouldn’t disappoint because it’s <b> A BRANDON SANDERSON BOOK</b> . His name alone is guarantee.<br/><br/>Although this book is only 88 pages (sooo shoooort), it’s still as awesome the way a S</span>
  <span id="freeText15772200206367312959" style="display:none"><b>Why so shoooort?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440455796ra/15977126.gif" width="370" height="274" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Legion is a short story about Stephen Leeds who has multiple aspects. <br><br><b> <i> My name is Stephen Leeds, and I am perfectly sane. My hallucinations, however, are all quite mad.</i></b><br><br>I’m a Sandersonitis for life and when I saw this book in a book sale, I immediately grabbed it. (Of course I paid for it.) I know this book wouldn’t disappoint because it’s <b> A BRANDON SANDERSON BOOK</b> . His name alone is guarantee.<br><br>Although this book is only 88 pages (sooo shoooort), it’s still as awesome the way a Sanderson book goes.<br><br>The banter between Stephen’s hallucinations are hilarious.<br><br><b>
  <i>” You may approach His Majesty,” Armando said. He stood at his window. Which was triangular-he occupied one of the peaks of the mansion. He’d demanded the position.<br><br>“Can I shoot him?” J.C asked me softly. “You know, in a place that’s not so important?A foot, maybe?”<br><br>“His Majesty head that,” Armando said in his soft Spanish accent, turning unamused eyes our direction.</i>
</b><br><br>And…<br><br><b>
  <i>”Can I shoot <i>her</i>?” J.C asked.<br><br>Ivy rolled her eyes. “Remind me why we keep him around?”<br><br>“Rugged good looks,” J.C. said.</i>
</b><br><br>Really, I love everything about this book. The mystery, the characters (even if some are just hallucinations) and just pure old Sanderson.<br><br>Time for book 2..<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438615057ra/15734921.gif" width="500" height="219" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15772200206367312959" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3021880153739010459">I've read this short contemporary fantasy novella multiple times and it is always an entertaining read. In this story Stephen Leeds, AKA 'Legion,'and his multitude of 'aspects' are hired to track down the missing inventor of a potentially magical camera, which has the ability to take photos of the past. Stephen is a very likable character and he uses the knowledge gleaned from his various aspects to help him solve the case. <br/><br/>The best part of this has to be the witty banter between Stephen and his</span>
  <span id="freeText3021880153739010459" style="display:none">I've read this short contemporary fantasy novella multiple times and it is always an entertaining read. In this story Stephen Leeds, AKA 'Legion,'and his multitude of 'aspects' are hired to track down the missing inventor of a potentially magical camera, which has the ability to take photos of the past. Stephen is a very likable character and he uses the knowledge gleaned from his various aspects to help him solve the case. <br /><br />The best part of this has to be the witty banter between Stephen and his various aspects. <br /><br />I loved the mystery, humor, and fast pace of the story. The ending was very intriguing and has left me eager to read the sequel.<br /><br />Rating: 4 stars. <br /><br />Audio Note: Oliver Wyman is a fantastic narrator who has no problems providing distinct voices Stephen and all his aspects. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7713597812150023475"><b>30/8/19: Full review up</b> <br/>This is only my second book/novella (never will be a fan of that word) from Brandon Sanderson and I think I am very impressed. My first one from him was Snapshot. Both are really short stories and both are not from the genre that he is considered to be best at. And yes, the selection of this has been methodical. Why, you ask? I’ll tell you why. I have been hearing so much spectacular shit about this author and about how he can do no wrong that I was finding it hard to bel</span>
  <span id="freeText7713597812150023475" style="display:none"><b>30/8/19: Full review up</b> <br />This is only my second book/novella (never will be a fan of that word) from Brandon Sanderson and I think I am very impressed. My first one from him was Snapshot. Both are really short stories and both are not from the genre that he is considered to be best at. And yes, the selection of this has been methodical. Why, you ask? I’ll tell you why. I have been hearing so much spectacular shit about this author and about how he can do no wrong that I was finding it hard to believe and intimidating at the same time. So I thought to sample out his work. And so far, I must say I am really impressed. I loved Snapshot and I loved this one too!<br /><br />This is so wonderfully woven for such a short story and I found the “characters” amazingly well-crafted in such a short time. They all felt different and had a personality of their own. The book maintained a very good pace and keeps you engrossed and it’s witty.<br /><br />Overall it has great entertainment value for the kinda short read it is and this has convinced me to finally pick up bigger works from Sanderson and hopefully, I will be rewarded bcz goddammit I need good fantasy in my life right now! <br /><br /><br /><br /><b>26/12/18:</b> RTC</span>

<div id="review_2959037659" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2959037659" />
    <a title="David" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/155663-david"><img alt="David" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581956036p2/155663.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2959037659?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="David" class="user" itemprop="url" name="David" href="/user/show/155663-david">David</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/155663-david?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/155663-david?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/155663-david?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/155663-david?shelf=psychology">psychology</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2959037659" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8654598383669009773">I've enjoyed reading Brandon Sanderson's <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6604209.Mistborn_Trilogy_Boxed_Set__Mistborn___1_3_' title='Mistborn Trilogy Boxed Set (Mistborn, #1-3) by Brandon Sanderson' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mistborn Trilogy Boxed Set</a> series, and since they are so imaginative. So, I tried this book by Sanderson, and I was completely surprised by the inventiveness and imaginative that went into <i>Legion</i>. Rather than inventing a whole new world as in the Mistborn Trilogy, Sanderson has developed a different type of person. Stephen Leeds, the main character, has a mental disturbance that causes hallucinations. He has a stable of about 50 different hallucinatory ch</span>
  <span id="freeText8654598383669009773" style="display:none">I've enjoyed reading Brandon Sanderson's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6604209.Mistborn_Trilogy_Boxed_Set__Mistborn___1_3_" title="Mistborn Trilogy Boxed Set (Mistborn, #1-3) by Brandon Sanderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Mistborn Trilogy Boxed Set</a> series, and since they are so imaginative. So, I tried this book by Sanderson, and I was completely surprised by the inventiveness and imaginative that went into <i>Legion</i>. Rather than inventing a whole new world as in the Mistborn Trilogy, Sanderson has developed a different type of person. Stephen Leeds, the main character, has a mental disturbance that causes hallucinations. He has a stable of about 50 different hallucinatory characters. He sees and interacts with these characters as if they are real. And mostly, they try to help him. Subconsciously, each character thinks and reacts and guides Leeds in his activities. They are like having an encyclopedia in your head, teachers, psychologists, bodyguards ... so many different personalities and capabilities. So, Leeds earns his living solving "cases" where these abilities are useful.<br /><br />Brandon Sanderson has managed to invent a type of mental disturbance that can be useful in certain situations. It can also be off-putting, such as preventing Leeds from going out on dates--his dates usually run away after a brief encounter with him. Leeds is so quirky, and yet continuously tries to convince himself--and others--that he is sane. His definition of sanity is being able to control the situation, not letting his behavior get out of hand.<br /><br />There is a bit of science fiction here--a camera that can take pictures of the past. But I don't classify this book strictly as science fiction because it is not central to the book's theme. I would really classify this book as "psychology-fiction", because the mental disturbance is probably invented.<br /><br />This book is not a single story; it is a collection of a few stories, each about a different episode. The book certainly caught my imagination. But my advice is DO NOT READ THIS BOOK. Instead, LISTEN TO THE AUDIOBOOK!! It is awesome! Oliver Wyman narrates the book, a very demanding task. Each of Stephen Leeds' characters is a completely different personality, and Wyman brings each one to life. I really like the rendition of "Tobias", one of the characters in Leeds' hallucinations. The other characters are also wonderful. Listen to the audiobook!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8654598383669009773" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<span id="freeTextContainer14522255969626408416">I hate short stories and never read them and I really hated the start of this book and I don't know why ! Hahaha I guess I have massive expectations from Brandon Sanderson and this just didn't hit the spot for me from the start like his other books did.<br/><br/>Towards the middle of this book I worked out what was going on. It is a beautifully written story and the characters are hilarious. This type of fantasy just isn't for me so I didn't like it and won't read the next. But it really isn't a horrible </span>
  <span id="freeText14522255969626408416" style="display:none">I hate short stories and never read them and I really hated the start of this book and I don't know why ! Hahaha I guess I have massive expectations from Brandon Sanderson and this just didn't hit the spot for me from the start like his other books did.<br /><br />Towards the middle of this book I worked out what was going on. It is a beautifully written story and the characters are hilarious. This type of fantasy just isn't for me so I didn't like it and won't read the next. But it really isn't a horrible read and I do recommend it to people looking for something different. <br />So I give it 3 stars :)</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4hEg/ibOmt93HSC5FbdSwfCB4rKdODI4wPiQXzdztrYQ+aiyTDZw9ijWZmpH2b49TytU7KGpiAIDeApy+O/cDw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Z9Xw5Xp3aRLakdEtcu8WlUixdm+9plcsX7ljfx1sKwKVPXipEI+DO4Val/4ggfpp9xvAMYE37RacOflS0vBBuw==')})
  }
//]]>

The dictatorial Augurs—once thought of almost as gods—were overthrown and wiped out during the conflict, their much-feared powers mysteriously failing them. Those who had ruled under them, men and wo<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText1247595032569490960\" style=\"display:none\">It has been twenty years since the end of the war. The dictatorial Augurs—once thought of almost as gods—were overthrown and wiped out during the conflict, their much-feared powers mysteriously failing them. Those who had ruled under them, men and women with a lesser ability known as the Gift, avoided the Augurs\' fate only by submitting themselves to the rebellion\'s Four Tenets. A representation of these laws is now written into the flesh of any who use the Gift, forcing those so marked into absolute obedience.\n\nAs a student of the Gifted, Davian suffers the consequences of a war fought—and lost—before he was born. Despised by most beyond the school walls, he and those around him are all but prisoners as they attempt to learn control of the Gift. Worse, as Davian struggles with his lessons, he knows that there is further to fall if he cannot pass his final tests. \n\nBut when Davian discovers he has the ability to wield the forbidden power of the Augurs, he sets into motion a chain of events that will change everything. To the north, an ancient enemy long thought defeated begins to stir. And to the west, a young man whose fate is intertwined with Davian’s wakes up in the forest, covered in blood and with no memory of who he is…<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"1247595032569490960\" Диалого-монолозите носят само и единствено моите собствени разсъждения и са пряко отражение на морала и философията ми, а често отговорите на въпросите ви се крият някъде напред или назад. Темите са вдъхновени от мои собствени разговори с Кр. Буря, които са ни карали да се чувстваме безсмислени на света.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"9869063964131708030\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson">About Brandon Sanderson</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1394044556p3/38550.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/38550.Brandon_Sanderson">Brandon Sanderson
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer3676946912046051148">Brandon’s major books for the second half of 2016 are <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18714787.The_Dark_Talent' title='The Dark Talent' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Dark Talent</a>,</i> the final volume in Alcatraz Smedry’s autobiographical account of his battle against the Evil Librarians who secretly rule our world, and <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded' title='Arcanum Unbounded' rel='nofollow noopener'>Arcanum Unbounded</a>,</i> the collection of short fiction in the Cosmere universe that includes the Mistborn series and the Stormlight <br/>Archive, among others. This collection features <i><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul' title='The Emperor’s Soul' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Emperor’s S</a></i></span>
  <span id="freeText3676946912046051148" style="display:none">Brandon’s major books for the second half of 2016 are <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18714787.The_Dark_Talent" title="The Dark Talent" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dark Talent</a>,</i> the final volume in Alcatraz Smedry’s autobiographical account of his battle against the Evil Librarians who secretly rule our world, and <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28595941.Arcanum_Unbounded" title="Arcanum Unbounded" rel="nofollow noopener">Arcanum Unbounded</a>,</i> the collection of short fiction in the Cosmere universe that includes the Mistborn series and the Stormlight <br />Archive, among others. This collection features <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul" title="The Emperor’s Soul" rel="nofollow noopener">The Emperor’s Soul</a>,</i> <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28698036.Mistborn__Secret_History" title="Mistborn: Secret History" rel="nofollow noopener">Mistborn: Secret History</a>,</i> and a brand-new Stormlight Archive novella, <i>Edgedancer</i>.<br /><br />Earlier this year he released <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15704486.Calamity" title="Calamity" rel="nofollow noopener">Calamity</a>,</i> the finale of the #1 New York Times bestselling Reckoners trilogy that began with <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17182126.Steelheart" title="Steelheart" rel="nofollow noopener">Steelheart</a>
</i>.<br /><br />Brandon Sanderson was born in 1975 in Lincoln, Nebraska. As a child Brandon enjoyed reading, but he lost interest in the types of titles often suggested to him, and by junior high he never cracked a book if he could help it. This changed when an eighth grade teacher gave him <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/176268.Dragonsbane" title="Dragonsbane" rel="nofollow noopener">Dragonsbane</a>
</i> by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/10333.Barbara_Hambly" title="Barbara Hambly" rel="nofollow noopener">Barbara Hambly</a>.<br /><br />Brandon was working on his thirteenth novel when Moshe Feder at Tor Books bought the sixth he had written. Tor has published <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/68427.Elantris" title="Elantris" rel="nofollow noopener">Elantris</a>,</i> the Mistborn trilogy and its followup <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10803121.The_Alloy_of_Law" title="The Alloy of Law" rel="nofollow noopener">The Alloy of Law</a>,</i> <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1268479.Warbreaker" title="Warbreaker" rel="nofollow noopener">Warbreaker</a>,</i> and <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7235533.The_Way_of_Kings" title="The Way of Kings" rel="nofollow noopener">The Way of Kings</a>
</i> and <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11543195.Words_of_Radiance" title="Words of Radiance" rel="nofollow noopener">Words of Radiance</a>,</i> the first two in the planned ten-volume series The Stormlight Archive. He was chosen to complete <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6252.Robert_Jordan" title="Robert Jordan" rel="nofollow noopener">Robert Jordan</a>’s Wheel of Time series; 2009’s <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1166599.The_Gathering_Storm" title="The Gathering Storm" rel="nofollow noopener">The Gathering Storm</a>
</i> and 2010’s <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8253920.Towers_of_Midnight" title="Towers of Midnight" rel="nofollow noopener">Towers of Midnight</a>
</i> were followed by the final book in the series, <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1166599.A_Memory_of_Light" title="A Memory of Light" rel="nofollow noopener">A Memory of Light</a>,</i> in January 2013. Four books in his middle-grade <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/623976.Alcatraz_vs__the_Evil_Librarians" title="Alcatraz vs. the Evil Librarians" rel="nofollow noopener">Alcatraz vs. the Evil Librarians</a>
</i> series have been released in new editions by Starscape, and his novella <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12796771.Infinity_Blade_Awakening" title="Infinity Blade Awakening" rel="nofollow noopener">Infinity Blade Awakening</a>
</i> was an ebook bestseller for Epic Games accompanying their acclaimed <i>Infinity Blade</i> iOS video game series. Two more novellas, <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13452375.Legion" title="Legion" rel="nofollow noopener">Legion</a>
</i> and <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13578175.The_Emperor_s_Soul" title="The Emperor’s Soul" rel="nofollow noopener">The Emperor’s Soul</a>,</i> were released by Subterranean Press and Tachyon Publications in 2012, and 2013 brought two young adult novels, <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10137823.The_Rithmatist" title="The Rithmatist" rel="nofollow noopener">The Rithmatist</a>
</i> from Tor and <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17182126.Steelheart" title="Steelheart" rel="nofollow noopener">Steelheart</a>
</i> from Delacorte.<br /><br />The only author to make the short list for the David Gemmell Legend Award six times in four years, Brandon won that award in 2011 for <i>The Way of Kings</i>. <i>The Emperor’s Soul</i> won the 2013 Hugo Award for Best Novella. He has appeared on the <i>New York Times</i> Best-Seller List multiple times, with five novels hitting the #1 spot.<br /><br />Currently living in Utah with his wife and children, Brandon teaches creative writing at Brigham Young University.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3676946912046051148" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>

His ambitious, multi-volume epics (Mistborn, The Stormlight Archive) and Hugo Award-winning The Emperor\'s Soul have earned both critical acclaim and a substantial popular following. \n\nIn the Legion series, distinctly contemporary novellas filled with suspense, humor, and an endless flow of invention, Sanderson has revealed a startling new facet of his singular narrative talent. Stephen Leeds, AKA “Legion,” is the series\' hero, a man whose unique mental condition allows him to generate a multitude of personae: hallucinatory entities with a wide variety of personal characteristics and a vast array of highly specialized skills. \n\nThe third and final entry in the series, Lies of the Beholder, is perhaps the strangest, most unpredictable installment to date. \n\nThe story begins with two seemingly unrelated events: the disappearance of Armando, one of Stephen\'s many “aspects,” and an unexpected cry for help from Sandra, the woman who, many years before, helped him learn to live with his condition. These events lead Stephen, along with several of his aspects, to a sinister high-tech firm specializing in advanced methods of human incarceration. \n\nThe result is a visionary meditation on the mysteries of the human personality. Like the volumes that preceded it, Sanderson\'s latest is original, challenging, and utterly absorbing. In Stephen Leeds, a man constantly struggling to understand and control his own divided nature, he has created one of the most compelling heroes in recent popular fiction. Like the best of Sanderson\'s work, Lies of the Beholder is something special.
